English Newspaper Comments on Japanese Political Turmoil

The Rise of Nationalistic Movements - A Russo-Japanese War May Ultimately Be Inevitable - ▲ Reuters, London, 17th. The question of whether the extreme nationalistic movement in Japan, which led to the assassination of Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi, was inspired by Hitlerism or Fascism, or arose from the Japanese government's moderate stance on the Sino-Japanese dispute in Shanghai, is now receiving national attention in Britain. The Manchester Guardian carries an editorial today stating that Japan has reached a critical point in its internal development. Japan's political development has ultimately failed to keep pace with its economic development, as Japan, though a highly organized industrial nation, still has a government with many feudalistic characteristics. The paper also discussed Russo-Japanese relations, stating that if the current internal strife in Japan results in the establishment of a military dictatorship, a Russo-Japanese war may be unavoidable. The former Morning Post correspondent in Japan, Bickering, also published an article in this morning's paper, stating that the trend in Japanese domestic politics is strongly towards democracy. Even the Emperor's authority is almost religiously sacred, and the Japanese people will never tolerate a system containing overt despotism. The Times carried an editorial discussing the future of Manchuria, stating that Manchuria is racially and geographically a part of China. Japanese military and government officials should realize that assuming full responsibility for the area will inevitably lead to a heavy burden. The paper hopes that the Lytton Commission can propose a solution satisfactory to both countries. It also stated that Japanese troops in their operational areas will sooner or later inevitably clash with Russian troops. Although Manchuria may shine brightly in the future through Japanese development, it should be known that it is currently full of difficulties and dangers.

Ten American Warships Withdraw

The American destroyers stationed in Shanghai, Nos. 218, 219, 222, and 224, as well as submarines Nos. 36, 37, 39, and 41, were led by the cruiser USS Chaumont and withdrew yesterday due to the withdrawal of Japanese troops from Shanghai and the lack of need to remain there. They have already departed Shanghai.

The Takeover Committee Took Over Dacha Yesterday

Joint Committee Oversight - Japanese Troops Leave the Territory in the Afternoon - The Security Brigade Takes Over Defense - The Japanese troops stationed in Dacha have, as agreed, completely withdrawn before 1:00 PM yesterday. The takeover committee on our side sent takeover specialists Tao Xiaojie and Lu Fengpu to handle the takeover matters the day before. The takeover was completely completed at around 1:00 PM yesterday. However, the situation in that area after the disaster is bleak, and post-disaster matters need to be urgently addressed. Therefore, people in that area have already organized the Baoshan War Disaster Relief Association to focus on carrying out reconstruction work. The details are recorded as follows: - ▲ Investigation of Japanese Troops Stationed in Dacha - The total number of Japanese troops stationed in Dacha reached 3,000. Their defensive locations were divided into five places: (1) Baohua Temple, (2) Qianxi Elementary School, (3) Su family residence, (4) Sun Jingxi residence, (5) Pushan Villa. There were infantry, cavalry, artillery, and horse-drawn mountain artillery teams, and everything that should be there was there. When the front-line combat was intense, that place was the Japanese army's rear headquarters. Its headquarters was stationed in Baohua Temple, and it was presided over by Xing Xianyi, the first battalion commander of the 7th Infantry Regiment, who served as the commander of the Japanese military garrison in Dachang Town. - ▲ Takeover Committee Departs - Since the Japanese side decided to completely withdraw its troops stationed there by 1:00 PM on the 17th, the takeover committee on our side, in order to negotiate properly in advance, sent special envoy Tao Xiaojie, Lu Fengpu, the second district chief of Baoshan County, and others as takeover committee members to Dachang the day before to discuss takeover procedures. Tao and others arrived there at around 10:00 AM the day before and immediately visited Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi and Lieutenant Kitamura Masae to discuss takeover matters. Tao and others also went to Luodian that night to notify our police force that they must arrive in Dachang completely before 10:00 AM yesterday in order to take over defense immediately after the Japanese troops withdrew. Tao and others stayed overnight in Luodian that night and set off for Dachang with the Capital Security Brigade responsible for the takeover at around 9:00 AM yesterday morning. - ▲ Our Police Force Arrives at the Field - The force responsible for taking over defense in Dachang this time was a company of the Capital Security Brigade, totaling 150 people, led by company commander Zhu Huang. When they arrived at the Beishihe Motor Road Bridge in Dachang Town, they temporarily camped there. Takeover committee members Tao and Lu first went to the Japanese headquarters to notify our police force that they had arrived and to discuss takeover procedures. Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi decided to completely withdraw the Japanese troops before 1:00 PM in the afternoon. After 1:00 PM, our police force would be responsible for maintaining law and order, and it was decided that the Longlin Pagoda Temple in Dachang Town would be the location for our police force to station. After the negotiations were completed, Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi personally accompanied Tao and Lu to the motor road bridge to greet our police force. - ▲ Japanese Troops Withdraw in Batches - The Japanese troops in Dachang were sparse in number. They began to withdraw in batches from 9:00 AM yesterday morning. All horse artillery teams were completely withdrawn before 11:00 AM. Infantry battalions were also withdrawn in batches. Before 12:00 PM yesterday noon, more than 2,600 of the more than 3,000 troops stationed in Dachang had completed their withdrawal. The garrison locations, such as Qianxi Elementary School, Su family residence, Sun Jingxi residence, and Pushan Villa, had all been completely withdrawn. Only the Baohua Temple garrison headquarters still had more than 400 infantrymen stationed there for the final withdrawal. - ▲ Once a Misunderstanding Was Resolved - When our police force took over defense yesterday morning, Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi had a misunderstanding. When Xing Xianyi accompanied our takeover officials Tao and Lu to greet the Capital Security Brigade, Xing Xianyi suddenly expressed to committee members Tao and Zhu that the Capital Security Brigade's takeover was inconsistent with the agreed terms. The agreement stipulated that the withdrawn areas should be taken over by special police. The so-called special police referred to regular police. Now the takeover was by the Capital Security Brigade, which seemed to violate the agreement. At that time, the Japanese garrison commander spoke forcefully. After our special envoy Tao explained the meaning of special police, there was no stipulation about Beijing. After repeated explanations, Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi finally nodded without saying anything. He immediately led our police force to station in the Longlin Pagoda Temple in Dachang Town. Then the national flag carried by our security brigade began to fly over Dachang Town. - ▲ Joint Committee Oversight - Regarding the withdrawal of Japanese troops, according to the agreement, it must be supervised by the joint committee composed of China, Japan, and neutral countries. Therefore, when the Japanese troops withdrew from Dachang yesterday, military attachés from various countries on the joint committee and Japanese committee member Harada arrived at the Japanese garrison headquarters in Baohua Temple in Dachang at 12:15 PM. Our committee member Wen Yingyi arrived in Dachang at 12:30 PM and carefully inspected the town's surroundings. He then went to the Japanese garrison headquarters in Baohua Temple to meet with the Japanese military attachés and the military attachés from various countries. He was received by Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi, and they talked for a long time before ending at 1:15 PM. Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi immediately stood up and poured champagne, congratulating the military attachés from various countries, our committee member Wen Yingxing, and takeover committee members Tao and Lu. They then went outside to take several photos together. Finally, Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi and Japanese Lieutenant Adjutant Kitamura Masae also took a photo with the temple monk Zheng Yin to commemorate the occasion. It was already 1:30 PM. The last 400 infantrymen remaining in the temple had also completely withdrawn. Japanese military attaché Harada said goodbye first with the military attachés from neutral countries. Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi and Lieutenant Adjutant Kitamura Masae also shook hands and said goodbye to our committee members. At this point, the Japanese troops in Dachang had completely withdrawn. - ▲ Exchange of Documents for Japanese Troop Withdrawal - Before the Japanese troops withdrew, Japanese garrison commander Xing Xianyi, our takeover committee member Lu Fengpu, and Zhu Huang, the company commander of the Capital Security Brigade responsible for taking over Dachang, exchanged and signed documents as a ceremony of handover between the two parties. Each party held one copy of this exchange of documents. The original documents handed over to our side by the Japanese side are recorded as follows: (The commander of the Japanese garrison in Dachang handed over the land, buildings, materials, and security used by the Japanese army at 1:00 PM on May 17, Showa 7, and the committee member of the Republic of China takeover committee assumed responsibility for the protection and security of the people thereafter, and the Japanese army no longer bore any responsibility. Therefore, please committee members of the Republic of China confirm at 1:00 PM on May 17, the 21st year of the Republic of China, that the land, buildings, materials, and security used by the Japanese army near Dachang Town have been completely protected by the Japanese army, and after the Japanese army garrison commander in Dachang Town has handed over all the security, they will assume responsibility for the protection and security thereafter. The two parties have agreed and signed in Baohua Temple in Dachang Town. Japanese Army Garrison Commander in Dachang Town Xing Xianyi, Republic of China Takeover Committee Lu Fengpu, Capital Police Department Fourth Security Company Commander Zhu Huang. - ▲ Wen and Sun Inspect - Our committee member of the joint committee, Wen Yingxing, specially accompanied takeover committee members Lu Fengpu and Tao Xiaojie to Dachang Town to conduct a detailed inspection at around 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon. They inspected the entire town for a week and went to the Longlin Pagoda Temple, where our police force was stationed, to inquire about everything in detail. He returned to Shanghai at 2:15 PM. In addition, Sun Xiwen, the magistrate of Baoshan County, also went to Dachang in person at 10:00 AM yesterday morning to preside over the takeover matters and investigate the disaster situation to properly plan for post-disaster relief.

Page 5

Page 6

▲ Post-Disaster Matters in Dachang - The Dachang Town area covers 130 square miles, including 1 town and 28 villages, with more than 7,000 households and a population of more than 30,000. It is bordered by Baojia Bridge in the Zhenru District to the south, Miaoxing Town, Zhuyuan Dun, and Jinjia Wooden Bridge to the east, Nanxiang to the west, and Yuncao River to the north. The town is densely populated, with many shops and markets. When the Japanese army invaded, the area was the rear guard of our army, with more than 30,000 troops stationed there. Therefore, it attracted the attention of the Japanese, who sent bombers to drop bombs, destroying more than one-third of the town's houses. On March 1, after our army retreated to the rear defense, the area unfortunately fell under the iron heel of the Japanese army. Yesterday, during the takeover, the reporter from the China Eastern News Agency specially accompanied Wen Yingxing, our committee member of the joint committee, to inspect the broken walls and rubble, which were desolate at a glance. The once prosperous market had been reduced to rubble. According to takeover committee member Lu Fengpu, it is estimated that more than 30% of the houses in the area were bombed and destroyed, and more than 30% were burned after being occupied. The town suffered the most severely. However, when our army retreated, the residents fled one after another, so there were few who were killed. As for the villages, when the Japanese army set fire to the houses, those who escaped were brutally shot, and those who stayed were burned to death. The matter was so tragic that it was painful to hear. According to the current first-step investigation, more than 400 people have been killed. At the moment, the villagers are displaced and wandering, unable to return. The most urgent task is to handle post-disaster relief. Therefore, the Baoshan County War Disaster Relief Association has been launched to focus on handling local post-disaster matters. The Jiangsu Provincial Government has allocated 300,000 yuan to the three counties of Jiading, Taicang, and Baoshan for relief. Baoshan received 100,000, of which 30,000 has been designated for Dachang to carry out reconstruction work. However, the destroyed residential buildings and the planting of fields also need to be addressed urgently. Regarding agricultural relief, the provincial government has allocated 1,000 dan of cotton seeds, which have been distributed without remaining, but it is far from enough. The residents' houses have also been requested from the Shanghai Local Maintenance Association to raise donations to promote reconstruction as soon as possible. As for the rectification of roads and bridges, the dredging of city rivers, etc., the Construction Bureau has also been consulted to start separately. Before the Japanese army withdrew, they cut down many telegraph poles along the way. At this time of takeover, they should also be repaired immediately. In short, in the area of Dachang today, everything is waiting to be done, and it is really not allowed to delay. Mr. Lu also told reporters that Baohua Temple in that area is one of the major monasteries in Jiangsu Province, covering an area of 140 mu. Previously, our 78th Division was stationed there, so the enemy frequently bombed and dropped more than 100 bombs, all of which fell around the temple. The temple has remained intact to this day. According to the Japanese army after the incident, when the Japanese planes inspected in the sky, they looked at the temple from afar and saw it as a sea of smoke. When the bombs fell there, they were all blown away by the whirlwind, believing that the temple gods were uniquely spiritual. Therefore, after occupying it, although they used the temple as the garrison headquarters, they did not dare to destroy it. This is a near-myth, which may be credible and incredible. Before the Shanghai War, Dachang had only 12 county police officers, and everything in the area was maintained by the local security corps. Now the security corps members have been scattered, and it will take time to recover. The small number of 150 police officers seems to be insufficient to maintain it. It is planned to request the takeover committee to send more police force so that local law and order can be worry-free. ▲ Takeover Committee Press Release Yesterday, the Takeover Committee issued a press release announcing the takeover of Dachang Town, saying that Lu Fengpu, the second district chief of Baoshan, and special envoy Tao Xiaojie, returned to the committee this afternoon and reported that they had completely taken over Dachang Town at 2:00 PM today. All issues concerning the security and reorganization of the town after the takeover will be handled by the district chief, and he will urge the competent authorities to restore various businesses as soon as possible and start investigating the household registration at the same time. ▲ Gujia Town Has Been Taken Over The Takeover Committee received a report from Baoshan County Magistrate Sun yesterday, saying that according to the report, the Japanese troops in Gujia Town, which is under the jurisdiction of the third district of Liuhang in the county, withdrew on the 13th. The third team leader of the provincial police team, Zhao Zhiqin, was immediately dispatched, leading 10 long-term police officers, to meet with Chen Long, the acting director of the third sub-bureau, leading the police to the town, preparing until 12:30 PM, when the Japanese troops were completely withdrawn, and our police immediately entered and set up posts. ▲ Jiangqiao Has Also Been Taken Over The Municipal Public Security Bureau submitted to the Municipal Government yesterday, saying, "Submitting a document stating that the Japanese troops in Jiangqiao have withdrawn, and officials and police have been dispatched to restore the original state, and a document has been submitted to Your Excellency for review and record." According to the report of Bi Zhenhua, the director of the first office in the sixth district, "This office has found that the Shanghai War has ended, and the Japanese troops in the front are gradually withdrawing. The Japanese troops formerly stationed at the Jiangqiao Branch Office under the jurisdiction of this office completely withdrew at 3:00 PM on the 10th of this month. The inspector of the branch office, Yu Zuyou, contacted the gentlemen in the town to clean up the local post-disaster matters and ordered the inspector to lead the long-term police to Jiangqiao on the 12th to restore the original state and continue to work. In addition to reporting the details of cleaning up the post-disaster matters in another document, we should first report the restoration date to Your Excellency for review," etc. In addition to ordering the director of the office to supervise his subordinates to seriously clean up all post-disaster matters and report at any time, we should prepare a document and submit it, requesting Your Excellency to review and record. Respectfully submitted to Mayor Wu, Director of the Public Security Bureau Wen Yingxing. ▲ Scheduled Takeover of Baoshan The Takeover Committee also reported that Baoshan County Magistrate reported that on the afternoon of the 16th, he and Huo Shi, a special envoy of the committee, held a letter from Harada, a military attaché of the Japanese embassy, to Baoshan County to contact the Japanese troops stationed in the city to receive the city on a specific date. He met with Major General Maeda, the commander of the 6th Infantry Brigade of the Japanese Army, and Adjutant Uetani, who stated that the troops of the regiment planned to withdraw the troops stationed in Yangxing on the 25th of this month and then withdraw the troops stationed in Baoshan County on the 26th, asking our side to lead the police to each place the day before to prepare for the takeover. ▲ Contacting Yangxing for Takeover At 10:00 AM yesterday morning, the Takeover Committee sent Wang Qingtao, the first district chief of Baoshan, and Liu Yumen, a special envoy of the committee, with a letter to Yangxing to contact the Japanese garrison stationed there to discuss takeover matters and detoured to Luodian to send a letter to the Baoshan County Magistrate to discuss everything. ▲ Collecting Firearms and Ammunition from the War Zone The Public Security Bureau issued a notice yesterday, saying, "For the sake of notice, it has been found that in the war zone, people who have picked up and collected firearms and ammunition are the bureau. In order to eliminate future troubles and dangers, the bureau has previously announced that the presentation of receipts and rewards has been filed. Now that the police power in northern Shanghai will be gradually restored, the loss and preservation of all firearms and ammunition must not be small. It is necessary to reissue the announcement. Anyone who has picked up firearms and ammunition must submit them to the local management office for verification and transfer within seven days from the date of the announcement. If anyone dares to conceal the report after the deadline, once it is verified or reported by someone, they will be charged with illegally possessing military firearms and will never be tolerated. All should abide by this order, be careful." Director Wen Yingxing. ▲ Jurisdiction of the Peace Police Regarding the jurisdiction of the peace police, Mayor Wu of the Municipal Government issued an order to Lu Luyun, the captain of the Peace Security Brigade, yesterday, saying, "For the sake of following the order, the security brigade should be controlled and dispatched by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. In addition to the separate order, this order should be obeyed." In addition, Director Wen Yingxing of the Public Security Bureau was ordered, saying, "For the sake of knowing the matter, all security brigades transferred from Beijing to Shanghai to take over the withdrawal area should be temporarily controlled and dispatched by the bureau. In addition to the separate order, this order should be obeyed." ▲ Letter Requesting the Return of Road Property Regarding the traffic on the two railway bureaus, due to the Japanese side's failure to return the Wusong Machine Factory and other properties as soon as possible, the two railway bureaus have not been able to complete the full line repair. Yu and Wen, our members of the joint committee, have repeatedly negotiated with the Japanese side, but the Japanese side has not given a definite answer. Therefore, Yu Hongjun specially sent a formal letter to the Japanese members yesterday, requesting the Japanese side to return the property of the two railways as soon as possible. The letter also solemnly stated that the Japanese side confirmed in the small committee of the ceasefire meeting that even in the garrison area, it should not hinder the traffic of the two railways. In addition, he also sent a letter to Mr. Ke Ninghan, the chairman of the meeting, requesting him to urge the Japanese side to return the road property as soon as possible. After our side sent the letter, Japanese committee member Murai, representing Okazaki, expressed to our side that the railway machine factory, etc., could be returned in a short period of time. ▲ Exchange of Living and Dead Prisoners The China Eastern News Agency reported that the Japanese authorities had previously requested our side to find a way to transport the remains of Japanese soldiers who had died in battle in Taicang and other places and were buried there back to Shanghai and hand them over to the Japanese side. Our side proposed exchange conditions, saying that after the remains of the Japanese soldiers were found, 38 of our captured soldiers must be released at the same time. The Japanese side immediately agreed. Now, the two Japanese soldiers buried outside the South Gate of Taicang have been found by the county and specially hired a steamship to transport them to Shanghai yesterday. Our side notified the Japanese authorities to send someone to receive them as soon as possible and release our 38 captured soldiers immediately.

Zhenru Takeover Postponed

▲ Delays in Welcoming Trains on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway ▲ Zhenru, which was originally notified by the Japanese side to withdraw on the 20th, but yesterday the Takeover Committee received a notice from the Japanese side that due to shipping reasons, the takeover schedule was changed, and Zhenru was changed to withdraw at 12:00 AM on the 23rd, and the western part of the Jiangwan Town Railway was returned first at 11:00 AM on the 19th, so the Takeover Committee is scheduled to hold a meeting at the agency at 11:00 AM today (18th) to discuss preparations for taking over the area west of the Jiangwan Town Railway. At the same time, the opening of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway will also have to be postponed.

New Atmosphere After the Takeover

▲ National Flags Flying to See the Light of Day Again ▲ Municipal Government Announcements to Settle Refugees The jurisdiction of the Fourth District Headquarters of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau in Zhabei, south of Suzhou River, south of the railway, west of Zhejiang Road, and east of Guangzhao Road, as well as the territory of the First Branch and the Second Branch, has been taken over by our side after the withdrawal of the Japanese army. The city situation has gradually recovered. The details of various situations are recorded as follows ▲ Post Office Recovery The Zhabei District Post Office on Gonghe Road and the Postal Savings and Remittance Branch were reorganized by Director Zheng Yuanluan, leading the staff, the day before, and started working yesterday. It is temporarily stipulated that the office hours are from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM. There are a total of eight staff members and 24 mailmen. Ordinary letters, registered letters, and express letters in the received area are delivered as usual. However, ordinary letters have also been delivered to areas where the Japanese army has not yet withdrawn, while registered letters and express letters have been suspended to avoid errors. ▲ Household Registration Completed According to Wu Hefu, the director of the household registration section of the Public Security Bureau, there are about 20,000 households in the territory of the Fourth District Headquarters, about 5,000 in the territory of the Fourth District First Branch, and about 10,000 in the Second Branch, totaling more than 35,000 households. After being grouped and checked since the day before, the investigation has been completed tonight (17th) and is scheduled to start sorting out tomorrow (18th) to seek verification. As for the second step, investigation certificates will be issued and household registration plates will be ordered. ▲ Public Works Matters The Zhabei Licensing Office of the Public Works Bureau on Minli Road went to sort out the equipment yesterday by the director, Song Xueqin, accompanied by two inspectors and one clerk. The Zhabei Engineering Management Office of the Public Works Bureau went to sort out everything yesterday by the acting director, Zhou Zanbang, accompanied by three technicians and four foremen. ▲ Public Utilities Jiang Songxiao, the director of the street lamp management office of the Public Utilities Bureau, led workers and managers to sort out the street lamps since the day before and immediately sent workers to the received area to repair the street lamps. Because the damage to the street lamps was easy to repair, as of yesterday, more than 600 street lamps had been completely restored. The advertising management office on Zhongxing Road decided to temporarily move to No. 56 Minli Road to continue working as usual. The vehicle management office on Minli Road sent technician An Huan yesterday to sort out everything and is scheduled to start working today. The shipping management office on Guangfu Road sent staff to sort out the office and the ship inspection office yesterday to facilitate recovery. ▲ Investigation of Donating Households Liang, the director of the North City Taxation Office of the Finance Bureau on Minli Road, hired workers to clean up the destroyed equipment the day before and led the clerks to sort it out yesterday morning. At the same time, he sent investigators to follow the police of the Public Security Bureau to investigate the household registration to restore the work of collecting donations within days. The ship donation office on Guangfu Road sent staff to sort it out yesterday and is scheduled to recover at the same time as the taxation office. ▲ Residents Move Back The shops, restaurants, vegetable restaurants, and snack shops in the received area of Zhabei have sorted out their windows and are preparing to resume business. Residents moved back from the concession to carry luggage and equipment in an endless stream, and the Hengfeng Bridge was overcrowded. Although the shops have not resumed business, they all hung the national flag of the Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth. The Shanghai North Office of the Public Security Bureau has sent double or four posts to each main road, and all road posts have been completely restored. The police brigade patrols the received area, and the security is very strict. ▲ Municipal Government Announcement Yesterday morning, Mayor Wu Tiecheng posted an announcement to reassure the people, saying, "For the sake of announcement, since the January 28 Incident, Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, Zhenru and other places have successively become war zones. The people have suffered the pain of exile, and their huts have suffered the disaster of artillery fire. Nine out of ten houses are empty, and the essence is exhausted. Flesh and blood are scattered, and livelihoods are collapsing. This mayor has witnessed this with heartache and is extremely sad and angry. Now that the ceasefire agreement has been concluded, the Japanese army is withdrawing one after another, and the order is becoming more and more stable. The districts that were complete in the past will naturally restore their prosperity. In addition to immediately restoring the guard and properly planning for post-disaster relief, this announcement is combined with the announcement of the migration of the people. Those who come to return to their old homes, serve your fields, sweep away the atmosphere, and restore our old view, without any hesitation. You will see the prosperity of the restoration. This mayor has great expectations. This announcement, May 16, 21st year of the Republic of China, Mayor Wu Tiecheng.

Postal Workers' Save-the-Post Movement

▲ Representatives visited Chen Mingshu but still no resolution. ▲ Expedite the implementation of the Postal Base Consolidation Plan. The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union and postal workers' unions from all over the country have proposed a Postal Base Consolidation Plan and submitted it to the Ministry of Communications for adoption and implementation. However, after repeated submissions, the Ministry has not yet issued a definitive response to the plan proposed by the unions. Yesterday, the union sent representatives to visit Minister Chen Mingshu to present everything, but to no avail. The emotions of all postal workers in the union are becoming increasingly agitated. In recent days, postal workers' unions from all over the country have been continuously inquiring about the progress, and expressing that the plan is the only good strategy to save the post office and that, no matter what, they must insist on urging the authorities to realize it in order to seek the permanent consolidation of the postal base. The following is a record of the urgent telegram from the National Postal Workers' Union to the Ministry of Communications: Urgent, Respectfully addressed to the Ministry of Communications in Nanjing. Ever since the recovery of postal rights, the post office has been deteriorating day by day, with chaotic systems, the establishment of redundant agencies, and the misappropriation of postal funds, shaking the foundation of the post office. Looking back at the situation under Sir Kunde's management, one cannot help but feel heartbroken. Our association has long been determined to address the difficulties of the post office and to rectify and maintain it. The Postal Base Consolidation Plan jointly proposed by the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union and postal workers' unions from all over the country this time is a concrete rescue plan for the post office, obtained through years of research and verification. The Ministry of Communications should take charge of the consolidation of the post office and should have already made grand plans in its secret deliberations. The plan proposed by postal workers across the country this time should coincide with the Ministry's aim to maintain the post office. It seems that it should be accepted sincerely. Any further delay will only incite public anger. We are telegraphing with utmost urgency, awaiting orders. Sincerely, The National Postal Workers' Union.

Central Political Committee Revises

Principles of the Publication Law. The detailed methods will be reported by the Department of Finance and the Department of Real Property after consultation. In the future, we can only borrow and advance the money in installments, because the provincial treasury is indeed in difficulty. After receiving the telegram, the Silkworm Committee held a committee meeting in the afternoon and resolved to push Chen Zhanru, Hua Yinchun, Jiang Daoshan, and Ju Gushu, among others, to draft three measures for borrowing funds, returning and offsetting cocoon trades, and consolidating silk factories, and then submit them to the department for approval. Inspection Report of Shanhaiguan

▲ Japanese troops repeatedly spy on Jioumenkou and Shimenzhai

▲ The puppet Fengshan Railway is completely owned by the Japanese. This reporter met with local authorities in Shanhaiguan in the evening, who claimed that the Japanese military's request to suppress the activities of the Volunteer Army is not only aimed at Shanhaiguan, but also seeks to seize Jioumenkou and Shimenzhai. Honjo Shigeru, commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army, previously sent someone to Shanhaiguan, repeatedly demanding that Brigade Commander He allow Japan to send 国境監視警察 (border surveillance police) to be stationed in Jioumenkou and Shimenzhai. He did not agree to this. Even when the Japanese army pursued the Volunteer Army, they were not allowed to cross the border of Suizhong County. Unexpectedly, a few days ago, Japanese troops suddenly arrived at Lijia Fort, which is under the jurisdiction of Linyu County and is located in Hebei Province. The Japanese army has clearly invaded eastward. On the morning of the 11th, more than 400 Japanese soldiers went to Mayingzi to be stationed. According to reports from local refugees, the Japanese army fired live ammunition for about twenty minutes when they arrived in the village. From Shanhaiguan to Jinzhou, a large Japanese detachment is stationed in Suizhong. In recent days, many have been dispatched to Qiansuo and Qianwei. Because Jioumenkou is the throat of Yuguan, and if this place is lost, Yuguan will be shaken, our side has now dispatched troops to guard it. Japanese soldiers in Shanhaiguan have been conducting exercises in the South China Barracks for days. Fearing accidents, many residents near South China have moved into the city. Also, at 4 PM on the 10th, more than 80 puppet police officers, led by Captain Kinukawa Hitoshi (Korean) and Squad Leader Guan Zongxian (Chinese), conducted drills outside the southeast corner of the city wall and fired live pistols. The residents were panicked. Because the police had previously declared that they were protecting the road, but their actions had gone too far, Brigade Commander He has lodged a serious protest with the Japanese garrison commander, Matsushita Shigetoshi. In response to the Japanese army, fearing that it would use the pretext of various dangers to overseas Chinese, we have organized a special police force to be responsible for the Nan Guan area. In the future, the station will also be managed by this police force. The Ninth Brigade is responsible for the security of the city. The special police serve as a buffer between the Chinese and Japanese troops. It is verified that the police were all selected from Linyu County. There is a post every two to three hundred steps. The captain is concurrently the Public Security Bureau Chief, Chen Baoshen.

This reporter then returned to the station to investigate the organization of the puppet Fengshan Railway. The General Bureau of the railway is located at the Liaoning Main Station. Shanhaiguan has a Chief of General Section in charge of traffic matters. There are two daily trains from Shanhaiguan in the morning and evening. One goes to Jinzhou, and one goes directly to Shenyang. There is a train commander (Japanese) on the train. All passengers must be inspected at the major stations of Suizhong, Jinzhou, and Goubangzi. Japanese inspectors grope young women's breasts and lower parts, while Japanese soldiers laugh beside them. The impolite behavior is hateful. The puppet Fengshan Railway trains are those seized from the Beining Railway. The locomotives and passenger cars have been changed to Fengshan symbols. The passenger cars are green. The station masters at each station are Japanese, and the deputy station masters are Chinese. The Japanese station masters are stern and harsh to their subordinates. If they are slightly displeased, they will punch and kick them. A certain Zhang, the deputy station master of Dagushan, released the westbound train two or three minutes early on the 8th of this month. The Japanese station master slapped him hard and ordered him to run on the platform for an hour. Zhang resigned in debt, but was arrested and imprisoned by the Japanese army. All railway telegrams and telephones are controlled by the Japanese station masters, and Chinese station masters are not allowed to interfere. Station accounting has been completely changed to Japanese characters. Of the puppet Fengshan Railway branch lines, only the Yingkou branch line and the Jinchao branch line can operate. The rest have not yet been restored. As for the puppet Fengshan Railway's consignment of passengers' luggage, in addition to collecting freight per piece, the Japanese station master must also pay an additional two jiao (small coins) per piece of luggage. This money goes into the Japanese station master's private pocket. A small number of the puppet Fengshan Railway police are former police from the Beining Railway, and the majority were recruited in Shenyang. The puppet Fengshan Railway porters have also changed into new-style vests, with a red circle of cloth embedded in the middle, inscribed with the English initials of Fengshan and numbers. At 8:40 PM, the puppet Fengshan train arrived from Shenyang to Shanhaiguan. Most of the passengers are working-class people. Only one first and second class passenger car is attached, and no one cares. The passenger cars are plastered with Honjo Shigeru's proclamations and proclamations from the puppet railway bureau. Honjo's proclamation advises farmers not to join the Volunteer Army, and the language is extremely comical. When the passenger car arrives at Shanhaiguan Station, the puppet police board the train to inspect it. Before the various trains of the Beining Railway depart, the puppet police also patrol with guns, paying close attention to the passengers. After the reporter completed his inspection, he took the Beining train back to Beiping that evening. However, a police officer followed him. In the first-class compartment, the Japanese army openly opened the door to inspect. The Shanhaiguan station of the Beining Railway is managed by a foreign employee, Corbin. Due to the Japanese military's disturbances, Corbin moved his office to a small foreign building next to the station to avoid their arrogance. In summary, the situation in Shanhaiguan is already extremely tense. (12th) Central Aircraft

(15th) Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Border

Establishment of a General Headquarters for Suppressing Communists

▲ Zhu Peide appointed commander, headquarters established in Hankou

▲ Troops stationed in the border areas of the three provinces are under his command. According to communications from Hankou, the 伪第四军 puppet Fourth Army led by Kuang Jixun in the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui border areas is the most valiant. In recent years, the counties of Guangshan, Luoshan, Huangchuan, Shangcheng, and Gushi in Henan Province, Huangpi, Huang'an, Macheng, and Huangmei in Hubei Province, and Huoqiu, Yingshan, Huoshan, and Taihu in Anhui Province have all been ravaged. Government troops have also repeatedly suffered defeats in suppression campaigns, such as the capture of Yue Weijun and the death in battle of Zhao Guanying. The arrogance of the bandits is self-evident. After the fall of Huang'an, the bandit's new base was successfully established again. Thus, it can spy on Xinyang to the north, damage the Pinghan Railway, and take Wuhan to the south, intending to occupy the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. The situation is serious, almost more so than in the past. Initially, the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Border Pacification Commissioner's Office was established, with Li Mingzhong as the commissioner. The troops under his jurisdiction included the four divisions of Ji Ren, Yu Xiang, Ge Yunlong, and Xia Douyin. Ji Ren pursued, and Yu intercepted. After years of bloody battles, the bandit's momentum was slightly curbed, but it was impossible to thoroughly eliminate them due to the deep mountains and dense forests. Later, Ji Hongchang left his post, and Li also had internal problems. In January of this year, Li resigned, and the Pacification Commissioner's Office was abolished at the same time. The suppression of bandits in the border area was without a dedicated official responsible. In April, the Hubei Pacification Commissioner's Office sent representatives to Beijing to visit the Military Affairs Committee, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, to report on the military affairs of bandit suppression in Hubei Province and suggested that a senior official be appointed in the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui border areas to be responsible for overall supervision and suppression. After considering for a long time, Chiang believed it was necessary, so he decided to appoint Zhu Peide as the General Commander for Communist Suppression in the Henan, Anhui, and Hubei Border Areas. The headquarters will be established in Hankou, and all troops stationed in the border areas of the three provinces will be under his command. The 88th Division of Yu Jishi, which previously resisted Japan in Shanghai, has also been dispatched to assist. Zhu is currently the Director of the Office of the Military Affairs Committee and Director of the Third Department, and he will not be replaced. Once he finds someone to act on his behalf, he will come to Hankou to invite the military authorities of the three provinces to hold a military conference to decide on a concrete plan for bandit suppression, and then issue a mobilization order. It is expected that the bandit suppression will become more active in the future.

Hubei Province Actively Clearing the Countryside

▲ The Countryside Clearing Promotion Association holds a membership meeting

▲ Requesting military and political organs to recover the fees apportioned to the gentry and wealthy. According to communications from Hankou, the Hubei Countryside Clearing Promotion Association has been established for quite some time and bears the greatest responsibility for raising funds. At the beginning of the association's establishment, it stipulated that the post-bandit suppression expenses would be 10 million yuan, with five methods of raising funds: (1) collecting salt surcharges, (2) increasing land taxes, (3) collecting business protection donations, (4) issuing post-disaster public bonds, and (5) fines from banning opium in various counties. The fifth item is negligible. Items two and three are also difficult to implement. Only items one and four are sufficient to supplement. However, the collection of salt surcharges has not yet been approved by the central government. Recently, after negotiations between the Pacification Office and the Hubei Coast Salt Affairs Audit Office, they have agreed to allocate 150,000 yuan per month. The item of bandit suppression public bonds totals 3 million yuan, which is to be apportioned among the gentry and wealthy in the province with property above 20,000 yuan according to their grades. However, after the floods and bandit disasters in Hubei Province, the poor have long been buried in ditches, and many of the wealthy have scattered in all directions. It is uncertain whether such a huge amount of money can be raised as scheduled. In order to facilitate bandit suppression, the association convened the second membership meeting on the 14th to discuss this matter. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Those gentry and wealthy who are apportioned public bonds and fail to pay within the deadline or refuse to accept letters of recommendation for public bonds shall be submitted to military and political organs for assistance in recovery. (2) If the gentry and wealthy believe that the amount of the purchase is inconsistent with their property, after verification, they shall be recommended for subscription according to their actual property. (3) The salt tax surcharge will continue to be strongly advocated to the central government, and 200,000 yuan per month will be allocated from the salt tax items for bandit suppression expenses until the day the bandits are cleared. Many people attended the meeting that day. He Chengjun, Xia Douyin, Kong Geng, Li Shucheng, Ye Peng, and others participated. Xia and He both gave speeches. Xia said that bandit suppression has made progress recently, but no one has handled the aftermath of each recaptured place. He hopes that the gentry and elders living in Wuhan will return to their hometowns, lead the people, and jointly seek to recuperate. He said that the bandit suppression in Hubei Province has been approved by the central government, and two more divisions have been transferred to assist, which can be deployed soon, and the strength can be said to be substantial. He hopes that public bonds will be raised as soon as possible so that it can progress smoothly. As for the discipline of the troops, it must be rectified, and it must be strictly corrected by orders. In addition, regarding the matter of borrowing one million yuan from the banking community with municipal public bonds as collateral, it was previously agreed that He Baohua, the representative of the Pacification Office, Shen Zhaonian, the representative of the Provincial Government, and Zhou Xingtang, the representative of the Association, would be responsible for the negotiations. However, the conditions of the banking community were very harsh: (1) The amount of the loan was reduced to 400,000 yuan. (2) The 150,000 yuan per month promised by the Salt Affairs Office was designated as collateral. (3) The Clearing Association apportioned 720,000 yuan in public bonds to the banking community, canceling the original agreement, resulting in no results. Therefore, He and others also presented reports at the general assembly meeting, and all agreed that they could not accept it, so it was agreed to hold another meeting that night to discuss it in detail. It is heard that it will be decided to abandon this loan and borrow from Jin City, Nonggong, and Provincial Banks. It is expected that it can be established after further negotiations. (May 14th)

Jiangsu Provincial Government Rectifies Land Tax

The Regulations for the Organization of the Land Tax Rectification Committee of Jiangsu Province have been passed by the Provincial Committee Meeting. They are now recorded as follows: (Article 1) The purpose of these measures is to rectify land tax and eliminate accumulated malpractices. (Article 2) The Land Tax Rectification Committee shall be jointly organized by one or two capable personnel from each office and department under the Provincial Government who are familiar with the land tax situation. (Article 3) The Committee shall rectify land tax in each county, starting with the county with the most serious accumulated malpractices, and the county shall be designated on a temporary basis. (Article 4) When the Committee arrives in a county, it shall first check the grain depot’s register of grain quotas, the household registers, and the tax collection registers to ascertain the exact amount of old arrears over the years, as well as the amount of grain depot collusion, both paid and unpaid, as a basis for investigation. (Article 5) In the case of old arrears, if it is found that the head of the grain depot and the tax collection officials have engaged in malfeasance, secretly collected taxes without remitting them, and the actual arrears are on the books of the clerks, the clerks should be immediately detained and ordered to make restitution within a deadline. If they resist detention and refuse to pay, their property should be seized and they should be severely punished according to the law. (Article 6) In the case of old arrears, if it is found that local bullies and gentry have resisted payment, and the actual arrears are owed by large households, the clerks should be instructed to truthfully provide a list of the names and addresses of the large households to the county, and military police should be dispatched, along with tax collection officials, to collect taxes from each household. If they still resist payment, they should be summoned to court for detention and pursuit, or their property should be seized for compensation. (Article 7) In the case of old arrears, in addition to the depot clerks and large households, there are also scattered small households with actual arrears owed by the people. The tax collection officials of each village should be instructed to summon the village heads to the bureau to report the true names and addresses of each taxpayer, and pursue payment from each household. If they intentionally conceal information and refuse to truthfully report, the village tax collection officials and village heads should be immediately dismissed and sent to the county for strict punishment. (Article 8) If the head of the grain depot in each county is found to have engaged in malfeasance and embezzled a large amount of national tax revenue, and the circumstances are serious, the Committee should submit a special report to the Provincial Government and dispatch police to escort him to the province for strict punishment according to the law. (Article 9) When the Committee members go to the counties to serve, they shall be paid travel expenses according to regulations. (Article 10) The expenses for rectifying land tax shall be paid from the item of overdue fines. (Article 11) These measures shall be promulgated and implemented after being decided by the Provincial Government Committee.

The Silk Industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Gradually Becomes Active

In recent months, due to the sluggishness of the world economy, silk prices have plummeted, and finance has stagnated. The silk inventory in Shanghai has reached more than 20,000 bales, and the silkworm cocoon inventory has reached more than 100,000 piculs. Silk and cocoon operators have suspended operations due to capital losses, and silver firms have stopped lending due to the falling value of collateral. A few days ago, the Ministry of Industry and the competent authorities of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces convened various related industries in Shanghai to hold a silk and cocoon relief conference, and resolved to exempt raw silk exports from taxes and subsidize each picul by one hundred taels. The Shanghai silver firms also believe that silk sales are of great importance to finance, and have continued to provide loans as much as possible. In the future, cocoon market activities and the resumption of work in silk factories are expected. Now, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Industry believes that the province's silkworm industry is prevalent in the south of the Yangtze River, and it is difficult to achieve universal loan issuance in Shanghai. It specifically instructed the county governments and chambers of commerce of Kunshan, Wuxian, Wujiang, Jintan, Danyang, Wujin, Wuxi, Jiangyin, Changshu, Yizheng, Jiangdu, Gaoyou, Baoying, Jiangning, Zhenjiang, Jurong, Huaiyin, Lianshui, Yixing, Liyang, Jingjiang, Songjiang, Nantong, and Haimen to instruct the silver and money industries to cooperate with silk and cocoon merchants and help each other when spring cocoons are on the market in order to maintain the silkworm industry. According to a Hangzhou dispatch, the silk and cocoon industries in Zhejiang Province have also become pessimistic since being affected by the Shanghai war. In order to relieve the silk and cocoon industry, the Zhejiang Provincial Government has formulated five measures and submitted them to the Political Committee for deliberation and implementation. Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Department of Construction, went to Shanghai a few days ago to attend the joint meeting of the authorities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces, and achieved satisfactory results in relieving the silk and cocoons of various provinces. The Hangzhou silver and money industry has organized a loan committee on the second floor of the Bank of China. Cocoon merchants in various counties and silkworm farmers in rural areas can directly borrow money. The provincial government also proposed resolutions on the 483rd committee meeting of the Finance and Construction Departments, resolving to set the maximum and minimum cocoon prices from 15 yuan to 30 yuan, and the cocoon drying fee shall not exceed three yuan. The municipal and county governments have been ordered to announce this to the public. The Hangzhou Municipal Government has also persuaded the cocoon merchants in Hangzhou to collect new posts from the Department of Finance and set up cocoon collection agencies. The cocoon agencies in Linping, Pingyao, Jianqiao, and Tangqi and other towns have all started weighing cocoons on the 16th. Yesterday, farmers who picked cocoons for sale were already on their way. This year, all cocoon agencies are using new weights. The purchase price of 100 catties of fresh cocoons is about 30 yuan. However, only Qingcheng is a silk weaving factory in the urban area that collects cocoons. (May 15)

▲The Tragic Situation of Disaster Victims in Jiangdu County In the Touxinqiao Township of the third district of Jiangdu County, due to the floods last year, there was no autumn harvest. The cries of the hungry were everywhere. Later, the disaster relief association witnessed the tragic situation and allocated some wheat flour to the township to provide temporary relief to hundreds of thousands of disaster victims. Unexpectedly, the spring famine this year is even worse. The disaster victims are all digging reed roots and river grass to fill their hunger, and recently they have even reached the point of starvation. This tragic situation is truly unbearable to witness. Now, in the blink of an eye, it is time to plant autumn crops, but it is difficult to raise funds for labor and seeds. If no measures are taken to provide relief, then there will be no hope for the autumn harvest this year.

Letter from Gao Keji

To the esteemed editor, I was astonished to read the news in your newspaper on May 14th, "A Tragedy Occurred in the Nanhui Election Committee." It has been found that Keji received a public letter from the Nanhui County Security Committee, ordering him to investigate the case of Chen Eyi and others, citizens of the sixth district, accusing Chen Xinyi, the head of the district, and Tang Yaoyu, the head of the jia, of illegally detaining, tying up, and injuring them. On the morning of May 10th, he took the first patrol boat of the police team sent by the county government with 12 policemen to Liuzhao Town. As soon as they arrived at the pier of the town's steamer, they saw Tang Yaoyu, Ji Qingren, Lu Da, Zhang Yongmei, Zhang Peilin and others leading many people with guns gathered on the shore. In an instant, they swarmed off the boat, forcibly twisted and dragged Keji ashore. Tang Yaoyu, Ji Qingren, Lu Da and others directed the rioters to open fire, beat Keji, and imprisoned him. The firearms carried by the accompanying policemen were also snatched away. The Zhuhai Security Team heard the alarm and came to rescue them, but their weapons were also confiscated, and three members of the team were captured. Fortunately, the county government continued to send a police team, a water patrol team, a guerrilla team, and policemen to rescue them in time. The above is Keji's situation of being beaten and imprisoned when he went to the sixth place to investigate the case that morning, which has nothing to do with the party headquarters election. The content of your newspaper is inconsistent with the facts. I am writing to request a correction in order to avoid confusing rumors. I sincerely hope so. Gao Keji, May 14th

Local News

Account of the French Mail Ship Fire

▲First-class Ship George Philippar

▲Machine Exploded, Ship-Wide Electrical Failure

▲Total Loss of Two Million Dollars

The newly built, most modern, first-class mail ship George Philippar of the French Mail Ship Company, after its completion, came to Shanghai for the first time. On April 23, it sailed back to its home country from this port. Unexpectedly, when it reached the Red Sea, near the port of Athens, the ship's hull suddenly exploded, and the entire ship caught fire. Many passengers were in distress, and even more sailors were killed. The ship was almost completely destroyed, with a loss of approximately $20 million. This is truly the greatest tragedy in the maritime world in recent times. The details are recorded as follows:

▲Elegant Ship Hull

The ship is the best and largest new mail ship of the French Mail Ship Company. The elegance of the passenger cabin layout, and the magnificence of the reception hall and dining room, are almost like a royal palace. According to the company's statement to reporters yesterday, the ship's large dining room is the first in Europe in terms of its magnificence and grandeur. The cost of the decoration at that time was 1 million francs, and the furnishings in the hall were mostly valuable antiques. The total cost of the ship, as confirmed yesterday, was 80 million francs, equivalent to 10 million taels of Shanghai silver.

▲Details of the Accident

Last year, the French Mail Ship Company built two new 24,000-ton, high-speed mail ships, using electric steam power, capable of traveling 19 nautical miles per hour. One was named Phil Croesus, and the other George Philippar, both assigned to the China-France line. The ship's maiden voyage to Shanghai coincided with the aftermath of the Great War in Shanghai. On April 23, it made its first trip from Shanghai to Marseille. Many passengers boarded the ship for Europe. On the afternoon of the 15th of this month, the ship arrived in the Red Sea, near the port of Athens, off the coast of Soumailli. Suddenly, an explosion occurred in the engine room. Because it was powered by electricity, the fire quickly spread throughout the ship, and the situation was particularly fierce. Captain Vick urgently sent a wireless call for help, and at the same time released lifeboats to rescue passengers.

▲Passengers Rescued

This time, the ship was carrying a total of 950 passengers to France, of whom 135 disembarked from Shanghai, mostly Westerners, with only a few Chinese, such as Wang Jun and Mrs. Shen Wang. Westerners, such as Mr. Mazzalron, the manager of the French Tram Company in Shanghai, also took this ship back to their country. After the accident, two British ships and one Russian ship first sailed to rescue the passengers. It has been reported that about 600 people have been rescued by British and Russian merchant ships. It is still unclear whether the remaining 300 people were rescued by other ships or went missing, as there have been no further reports. Among the passengers on board this time, most of those who departed from Shanghai were French naval officers, and a team of French naval soldiers withdrawn from Shanghai also took this ship back to their country. This time, they all suffered the same fate.

▲Russian Ship Rescues

The National News Agency's Aden dispatch on the 17th stated that a wireless message was received today stating that a Soviet Russian ship carrying 420 passengers and crew members rescued from the George Philippar was sailing here. In addition, it has also been confirmed that among those who escaped danger, three have died and several have suffered severe burns. It is now feared that the total number of deaths and injuries, after combining reports from various sources, will far exceed this number.

▲Rescued Passengers

Reuters' Athens dispatch on the 17th stated that the Kandelaker carried over 128 rescued people, including 66 passengers, 15 soldiers, 22 sailors, and 25 seamen. It will arrive here at 3:00 p.m. today. The Masut carried 125 rescued people, including 39 French passengers, 16 children, 5 natives, 11 naval soldiers, 3 crew members, and 51 Chinese seamen. It will arrive here at 5:00 p.m. The French ship Antrepont set sail at midnight yesterday to pick up the 420 people rescued by the other ship, and then transport them here, or send them to Jibouti.

▲Difficult Navigation in the Red Sea

The Red Sea is a very hot place, and navigation is very difficult. Five years ago, the company's mail ship Vindinapora also had an accident there. This time, when the George Philippar traveled to that place, the French Navy ship in this port received a wireless report stating that the cause of the accident was that the Red Sea was too hot, which caused an electrical explosion that spread throughout the ship. Therefore, although there were fire-fighting equipment on board, it was impossible to extinguish the fire.

▲Sharks Eat People

There are many sharks in the Red Sea, and they are all huge. Sailors warn each other against working when ships pass through, because if they fall into the sea, they will definitely be eaten by the sharks, and there is no hope of survival. This time, when the ship had an accident, many of the people on board who did not have time to get into the lifeboats and fell into the sea could not be rescued and were eaten by sharks.

▲Sailors Killed

Most of the firemen in the ship's stokehold were Chinese, totaling 19. At the time of the electrical explosion, these 19 firemen were unable to escape and were all killed by the explosion. It is said that none survived. A considerable number of sailors also failed to escape and were buried in the fire. The investigation is still ongoing.

▲Goods Completely Lost

The goods transported to Marseille and Paris from Shanghai on this ship included 214 pieces of Huzhou silk and silk waste, 210 boxes of tea, 59 pieces of valuable luggage, yarn waste, pig intestines, and dozens of pieces of groceries. A large amount of goods shipped from Japan, Hong Kong, and other ports to France was also on board. This time, the cargo hold was completely burned down.

▲Ship Hull Destroyed

The ship is still burning near Athens. Captain Vick has been rescued by a Russian ship. It is found that the captain was originally the captain of the Bourges ship. Last year, the Bourges ship caught fire and burned down in France, so he was reassigned as the captain of the new ship. Unexpectedly, he encountered a disaster on his first voyage. Now, the Shanghai office has received a telegram from the Athens branch, but the cause of the accident has not been reported in detail. However, it can be confirmed that the ship is completely destroyed. The total loss is estimated to be 20 million yuan.

▲Startling Questions

The National News Agency's Paris dispatch on the 17th stated that although there are many conflicting reports about the passengers on the French mail ship George Philippar, there is now good reason to believe that all of them are out of danger. As for the cause of the fire, it is still a mystery, and speculation has begun. It is still remembered that the ship was almost destroyed by fire not long after it was launched. Therefore, some people speculate that there are still weaknesses in its internal structure, which led to this major disaster. However, some also speculate that the negligence was due to someone else's conspiracy. It is said that before the ship set sail for its maiden voyage from Saigong, detectives boarded the ship for a thorough search. At that time, the authorities discovered a conspiracy, because the ship was transporting military supplies to Japan, and some people attempted to blow it up. Although the shipping company denied it at the time, and the detectives did not find any suspicious objects, it is speculated that there may have been an automatic explosive device hidden in the ship, which the detectives did not detect. However, because its timing mechanism was incomplete, it did not explode until the return voyage. Starting today

Suspension of Silk Export Tax

The National News Agency reports that, due to the recent decline in the silk industry, the government has established relief measures. According to reliable information, the export tax on white silk, gray silk, yellow silk, dougong silk, and waste silk listed in Nos. 180 to 184 of all export tariffs, as well as the special donation originally levied (i.e., the silk industry public debt fund collected by the Jianghai Customs), has been decided by the Ministry of Finance to be suspended from the 18th of this month, and all customs nationwide have been ordered to implement it uniformly.

Shanghai's Epidemic Prevention Efforts

▲ Yesterday, the authorities of the Chinese and foreign concessions held a meeting regarding the current outbreak of cholera in the city. The outbreak was discovered earlier this year than last. Liu Ruiheng, Director of the Department of Health of the Ministry of Interior, along with specialists Jin Baoshan and Yan Zhizhong, have already arrived in Shanghai. Yesterday, at 3:00 PM, they convened a formal epidemic prevention meeting at the Shanghai Port Quarantine Administration. All agenda items were fully discussed and have been submitted to the relevant agencies for prompt and effective implementation to benefit public health. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

▲ Meeting Details: Attendees included Hu Hongji, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, and Division Chief Wu Liguo; Jordan, Director of the Public Concession Health Department; Dr. Labo, representing the French Concession Municipal Council's Supervisor Fotianya; Wang Peiyuan, Chairman of the Chinese Red Cross; Yan Xiqing, President of the Chinese Red Cross General Hospital; Chen Yonghan, representing Zong Liande, Director of the National Port Quarantine Administration; Cheng Zhaiyi, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Health Laboratory; and Liu Ruiheng, Jin Baoshan, and Yan Zhizhong from the Department of Health, among others. Director Liu served as chairman. After the meeting commenced, the chairman gave a speech, stating briefly that the joint epidemic prevention work of the Chinese and foreign concessions last year, as well as the large-scale publicity efforts, had yielded very good results. Cholera has already been discovered this year, so efforts should be continued promptly to protect the safety of citizens' lives. Furthermore, most of the gentlemen present are old friends, which is especially valuable. He expressed his hope that everyone would contribute to the epidemic prevention efforts so that today's meeting can achieve satisfactory solutions.

▲ Resolutions: (1) Representatives from the Central Cholera Prevention Office, the Municipal Health Bureau, the French Concession, and the Public Concession reported on the results of last summer's epidemic prevention efforts. (2) All parties will cooperate to continue the following: A. Establish a Central Epidemic Prevention Headquarters in Shanghai to oversee all relevant matters, with the Department of Health supervising its progress. B. If an epidemic is discovered, the relevant agencies should promptly investigate the location where it occurred and the family's situation. At the same time, the joint headquarters must be notified to send personnel to inspect everything to prevent the spread of the epidemic. A subcommittee should also be established to investigate various epidemic diseases. C. Establish a subcommittee to organize lectures, films, and other written publicity methods. (3) Conduct epidemic prevention injections for all Shanghai citizens. Hu Hongji announced that the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau plans to inject at least one million people this year. The Public Concession and French Concession also expressed their willingness to assist as much as possible. The epidemic prevention vaccine for the Chinese concessions has been decided to be fully supplied by the Shanghai Health Laboratory. (4) Investigate, coordinate, and improve the equipment and resources of various hospitals in the city, as well as temporarily establish epidemic hospitals to provide places for preventing and treating epidemic diseases during the summer. (5) Conduct widespread inspection work, including several aspects: A. Inspection of fish, meat, vegetable foods, and drinking water. B. Sanitation and epidemic prevention work related to feces, and strict fly control in garbage dumps. (6) Epidemic prevention matters for transportation agencies such as seaports and railways will be assisted by the Shanghai Port Quarantine Station and the Ministry of Railways. All of the above major cases have been resolved. Each representative present was instructed to immediately notify their respective administrative agencies to be responsible for handling them separately.

Record of the Postal Remittance Bureau Supervisory Committee

▲ Song Ziwen and Chen Mingshu Both Attended. The regulations of the Supervisory Committee of the Postal Savings and Remittances Bureau were previously formulated and promulgated by the Executive Yuan. All seven committee members, excluding the Minister of Transportation, the Minister of Finance, the Minister of Audit, and the Director of the Postal Department as ex-officio members, the other three committee members were appointed by the Executive Yuan: Liu Shufan, Deng Ruiren, and Zou Minchu. The supervisory committee held its first meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at the Savings and Remittances Bureau. Minister of Transportation Chen Mingshu, Minister of Finance Song Ziwen, Minister of Audit Ru Yuli, Director of the Postal Department Long Dafu, and committee members Liu, Deng, and Zou (Deng Ruiren as proxy) attended. Minister Chen chaired the meeting, reporting on the establishment of the committee. Yang Jianping, Director of the Savings and Remittances Bureau, reported on the business conditions of the past two years, stating briefly that although the development of the bureau's business since its official establishment in March of the previous year has not been entirely satisfactory, the results have also been considerable. The bureau's main businesses are remittances, savings, and investments. The business operations of the past two years have all improved. For example, the total amount of remittance drafts issued in the 18th year (i.e., before the establishment of the bureau) was over 13.3 million, and in the 20th year, it increased to over 16.1 million. Previously, the annual increase was no more than 5 million, but now it has increased by nearly 30 million. There are four reasons why it has increased so sharply: (1) Adding domestic remittance bureaus and offices; (2) Increasing the amount of remittances; (3) Adding small amount remittance drafts; (4) Reducing remittance fees. Regarding savings, the total amount of savings in the 18th year was only over 11.8 million, but in the 20th year, it increased sharply to over 27.6 million. The main reasons for the sharp increase were (1) Restoring and increasing savings post offices; (2) Adding various types of savings; (3) Paying attention to publicity and convenient methods for depositors. As for investments, a prudent approach has always been adopted, and cash reserves are kept sufficient, usually above 40%. The types of investments are divided into four categories: (1) Domestic and foreign government bonds; (2) Bonds of the Shanghai, Hankou, and Tianjin Municipal Councils and various public utility companies; (3) Real estate; (4) Mortgage loans and overdrafts. All account statements have been reported to the ministry for record. The bureau has only been established for two years, and it has coincided with floods and wars, and the finances of various places have been sluggish. However, even with these results, the future is unlimited. I have only been in office for more than three months, and it has coincided with the military affairs against Japan, and the market is depressed. Therefore, I have to adopt a tightening policy for business. For example, unimportant employees in the bureau have been laid off. In the future, we must strive for prudence in investment. Because savings are the hard-earned money of the common people, entrusted to the bureau for safekeeping. I will definitely take the interests of depositors and the development of the national economy as the premise. Afterwards, Committee Member Liu Shufan proposed that the bureau's accounts be audited and publicized to strengthen public trust. It was resolved to entrust Chen Riping as the accountant of the committee to audit and publicize the accounts. Also, because the committee's affairs are important, Ru Yuli, Liu Shufan, and Deng Ruiren were jointly elected as standing committee members to handle various matters during the recess of the committee.
