A Discussion of the Recent Situation in Geneva (Part 2)

— Ji Ping

Outside the scope of the League of Nations, the public opinions of European and American countries have given us strong help, such as Soviet Russia and the Near Eastern countries of Turkey and Egypt. The United States is even more sympathetic. Even the South American countries of Argentina, Brazil, and Chile, these ABC countries, although they cannot compare with the powerful countries, their influence in South America is indeed not small. In terms of the public opinion of the 62 countries, both members and non-members of the League of Nations, it can be known that more than 50 countries in the world have expressed goodwill towards us. Therefore, in this Sino-Japanese dispute, our country has won the honor of absolute moral victory in the international community. However, honor is ultimately very empty. What we are asking for is practical gain. If the League of Nations ultimately cannot take effective sanctions against Japan and force it to return our land and compensate us for our losses, then why should our country harbor excessive dreams? In the past, the League of Nations could only say a few fair words. Whether it can invoke Article 16 of the Covenant to make Japan submit is still considered a question by the people in the League of Nations! Recently, Geneva has been crowded with officials and dignitaries, and diplomats from various countries are very active. There are currently four major conferences being held: (1) The League of Nations Administrative Assembly, which meets three times a year, with May being the regular session. The Sino-Japanese issue is of course listed as an important agenda item. (2) The League of Nations Committee of Nineteen, a specially established council specifically for studying the Sino-Japanese issue. (3) The Disarmament Conference. Due to the sudden outbreak of the Far East issue, countries are on guard regarding disarmament. It can be seen that the Sino-Japanese war has had a great impact. (4) The Opium Suppression Conference. Since the establishment of the puppet state after the occupation of the Northeast, it is said that there is a motion to monopolize opium, which has aroused enthusiastic attention from this conference. These four international conferences are all related to the Sino-Japanese incident, which shows the seriousness of the Far East issue. Our country is also concentrating its diplomatic efforts in Geneva. Mr. Yan Huiqing, Liu Wendao, Huang Musong, and Hu Shize are attending the above-mentioned four major conferences separately, negotiating and working hard. In fact, the ability of our country's representatives to operate in Geneva may even be better than that of Japan. However, diplomacy depends entirely on national strength. Without a strong government, a strong nation, and a strong army, navy, and air force as backing, no matter how diplomatic you are, it is in vain! Secondly, the diplomacy of a country must determine its diplomatic policy. For example, in interpersonal relationships, there is the so-called (moral friendship) or (friendship in adversity). Why should countries be an exception? Our country's diplomacy has never had a consistent policy, and sometimes it cannot avoid falling into an isolated situation. I hope that from now on, we can break through the difficulties of the national crisis, and then revitalize politics and strengthen national strength, so that we can win in diplomacy.

Filial Son Guo

— Zhang Wanlong

There was a man named Guo in Liuhe. His family belonged to the farming class. Plowing in spring and harvesting in autumn, the whole family relied on it for support. He had an old mother who was blind and sick, and she was bedridden all year round. Guo took care of her very carefully. Whenever there was something delicious, he would always offer it to her, not daring to keep it for himself. The villagers all praised him. Soon, the Japanese army invaded and attacked. Guo's residence happened to be in the line of fire. His wife said to him, "The enemy is deep. Why don't we take shelter?" Guo said, "My mother is old and blind, and walking is difficult. Taking her to flee would hasten her death. If I abandon her and seek survival for myself, would there be any reason in the world? Even if I am foolish, I would not do this." His wife said, "Then shall we sit and wait for death?" Guo said, "I will live with my mother, and die with my mother. I only seek peace of mind. What is there to fear about life and death?" Before long, the war broke out, and the artillery fire was very fierce. Bullets fell like rain. All the villagers took shelter, but Guo alone served his mother and lived happily. One night, a giant shell hit their house, burning the walls and collapsing the walls. The whole family died as martyrs. My relative, Mr. Ye, was Guo's neighbor. That night, he lingered in the village because of something. He witnessed their whole family's death. The death was extremely tragic. He survived the disaster and fled to Hangzhou, where he described the outline of the events to me. Therefore, I write it out to serve as a warning to those who have the heart of beasts. May they be alarmed when they read it. (Thank you for the reward)

The Disorganized Front Gate Fellow

— Ying

｜Miscellaneous Writings of the Old Capital, Part 2｜ Stepping out of the noisy and chaotic East Railway Station, filled with shouts and the smell of smoke, the first thing that caught my eye was the towering, massive, seemingly miraculous, yet familiar Front Gate tower. Then I saw the heads of people wriggling under the towering building, and the slowly moving streetcars. The streetlights shone brightly and humorously on the ground, and a tin hat was blown back and forth by the cold wind. At this time, the snow was falling even harder, and the toiling people covered their heads with a piece of cloth, without any fixed rules or direction, just like small insects on the water's surface weaving together. Only in the dark corner next to the station stood a large, black pile of rickshaw pullers. Under the threat of cold wind and snowflakes, they held bean-sized oil lamps and moved their wet, heavy footsteps, waiting for customers to hire them for labor. This towering, massive Front Gate tower is just like the one I saw in the picture, except that there are now a few more snowflakes, and a few fewer camels pacing slowly like poets in front of the tower.

Tixiangzhai Show Talk

Yang Qi (Part 2)

— Gan Yi

Earlier, Peifu's army was defeated and retreated to Wuchang. Wuchang Wutai Gate was built by Zhang Zhidong, the governor of Huguang at the end of the Qing Dynasty, with a capital of one million. Therefore, the seven counties of Xianning were spared from flooding. In the autumn of the Bingyin year, the water was two feet higher than the shore. Pedestrians were ankle-deep. A certain army occupied Hongshan, overlooking and attacking the city. Peifu crossed the river to Xiakou. In the evening, he talked with Qi in the room. His general Qian entered, saw Qi, and wanted to say something but stopped. He asked for paper and wrote a few lines to show Peifu. Peifu said, "This is not what I want to do." Qi said quickly, "Shall we breach the river to flood the enemy?" Peifu said, "Yes. How did you know?" Qi said, "Zi Wu had planned this with me. I repeatedly thought it was impossible." At this time, Qian looked at Qi and said, "Fortunately, keep it secret. Don't tell anyone else." Qian retired. Qi then said to Peifu in a serious tone, "If this gate is breached, the seven counties of Xianning will be submerged. There are nearly ten million people in the seven counties. There are only four thousand enemy soldiers. Is it not right to sacrifice the people of the seven counties for the sake of four thousand enemies? Moreover, the enemy is perched high on Hongshan, and the horizontal line is twenty or thirty feet above Wuchang City. Breaching the water will only be level with the river. I am afraid that the enemy will not be killed, but the residents will die. Both sides raise banners and troops, saying they are saving the people. I am not saving the people, but killing them. What is the reason?" Peifu was moved and stopped the plan. Qian's plan failed. Qian resented Qi very much. Later, Qian died in the Xiangfan rebel army. Qi is still healthy, eats well, and writes poetry. The way of heaven is believable and unbelievable, unbelievable and believable. Qi served Peifu and endured many hardships. As for Peifu's defeat, rise again, and defeat again, Qi left and went elsewhere. After three years of living with someone who was not the right person, he did not hold any position or make any suggestions. He took his beloved concubine, Di Meinan, and returned to the south. He settled in a garden and no longer had any desire to ask about the world. Qi's talent and knowledge are beyond the reach of ordinary people. He is not just good at poetry. His poetry is rich in the style of the Tang Dynasty. He has written a collection called "Jiangshan Wanli Lou." Our country's aviation industry began in the second year of the Republic of China. In the beginning, it was only used for military purposes. Yuan Shikai founded the Nanyuan Aviation School, with Qin Guoyong as the principal. At the beginning, the school had six aircraft, all purchased from Germany. The coaches were also all Germans. In the third year of the Republic of China, when suppressing the White Wolf, Qin and a certain coach each drove one aircraft to fly to Guangshan, Henan Province for reconnaissance. However, due to poor driving skills at that time, it was of little value in the military. The social elite also paid little attention to it. However, Qin's presence in China cannot but be regarded as a pioneer in the aviation industry. After the fifth year of the Republic of China, the aviation school once expanded to twelve aircraft. They were all purchased from abroad. Due to poor repairs, three or four aircraft were damaged after a while. When Zhang Zuolin extended his power to Beijing, he knew to value aviation very much. However, he only recognized the Northeast as his base, so he did not plan to expand the Nanyuan Aviation School. Instead, he took eight good aircraft from the school and transported them to the Northeast as the foundation of the air force. He also purchased a large quantity from the United States and Japan, and hired foreign instructors for active training. As a result, the Northeast Air Force was able to stand out in the country due to its quality and quantity. However, due to the dereliction of duty by the guards, the September 18th Incident ended up supporting the thieves and fueling the flames. The Nanyuan Aviation School, which had been destroyed many times, had long become a historical term. As for our country's civil aviation industry, it started with the Shanghai-Chengdu aviation service founded by the Ministry of Transportation in the seventeenth year. This is a recent event.

He turned his body around and strode away with a majestic and arrogant air.

Speech

Officialese, Part 4

— Fo

The Jiangsu Provincial Government has resolved to establish chief county magistrates in fifteen counties including Shanghai, Jiangning, Zhenjiang, Songjiang, and Taicang. There will be changes to the current county magistrates, and talent will be the standard. If interpreted according to the text of this passage, the previous fifteen county magistrates were not selected based on talent at all, which has already been publicly admitted. What is puzzling is that Jiangsu Province, with its sixty-one counties, originally had first-class, second-class, and third-class counties. Why is there now a new category of chief county magistrate? This is very strange. However, the scope of authority of the so-called chief county magistrate is unknown compared to that of the former first-class county magistrates. If the scope of authority is also the same as that of the first-class county magistrates, and only the name of chief county magistrate is changed, this is called (changing the soup but not the medicine,) why go to the trouble? Furthermore, the issue of talent cannot be identified solely through examinations, introductions, relatives, etc. It is necessary to test their performance before seeing whether they are talented or not. If so, is it possible that none of the fifteen counties has achieved satisfactory results in governance? It is unknown what kind of people the newly appointed fifteen county magistrates are, whether they will have amazing achievements that can be shown, which is also doubtful. Or it is said that the reason why the provincial government established the chief county magistrates is not like this, or there is another motive. However, the recent provincial government is unwilling to do practical work and instead focuses on making a fuss over superficial details, which is one example. This is officialese, part 4.

Expressing Resentment

— Zhu Fu

Who bears the responsibility for the border,

Opens the door to invite the thieves?

The rivers and mountains are stained with blood,

The golden walls have turned to ashes.

White bones vie for food with dogs,

Green forests echo with the cries of ghosts.

The sad wind rustles,

The setting sun shines on the city wall.

Hearing that the enemy has come to the homeland,

The slaughter has emptied the city.

On the day of the nation's survival,

In the midst of the mountains and rivers, I am filled with emotion.

In this life, I have encountered great chaos,

And I intend to join the army.

Where will this great catastrophe end?

I raise my head and ask the heavens.

Beacon fires rise continuously,

The enemy's atmosphere has not yet been cleared.

Luoyang sings and dances merrily,

Shanghai is filled with war-like sorrow.

Ants climb the chariot and weep,

Turtles go ashore and roam.

The southeast is lightly abandoned,

I weep and cry for the divine land.

The cream and blood have been extorted,

The common people cannot bear it.

Pretending to be mighty, they drive fierce tigers,

Plundering food to feed hungry eagles.

In broad daylight, they dance like demons,

In red mansions, they hate ghosts at night.

Towering old mansions,

Withered and fallen, like dead vines.

Science

Several Small Handicrafts

— Guan Han

Since the outbreak of the Shanghai War, the most significant tragedy has been the impact on countless refugees suffering unemployment. Besides employing the unemployed as much as possible, we should also impart knowledge of small-scale crafts to enable them to have skills to support themselves. Having seen this, I am presenting three or two minor crafts that I have researched and successfully developed, hoping to fulfill my responsibility.

(1) Flypaper

Ingredients: 4 ounces of rosin, 1 ounce of honey, 1 ounce of raw sesame oil.

Instructions: Put the above ingredients into a pot, heat to melt, and stir slowly with a stick to mix evenly. Then, spread it on thick hemp paper that has been soaked in glue.

(2) Mosquito Repellent

(A) Ingredients: 80% camphor alcohol (available at pharmacies), 20% denatured alcohol.

Instructions: Mix them evenly in a bottle, seal, and store to prevent leakage. If having an outdoor evening banquet, apply it all over your face, hands, and feet to avoid mosquito attention. Or, put a few drops on your pillow for a peaceful sleep without worry.

(B) Ingredients: Equal parts lemon juice, a little wine, and Zhenjiang vinegar.

Instructions: Mix them evenly in a bottle as before. Spray around the bedroom or damp areas to repel mosquitoes.

(3) High-Quality Tooth Powder

Ingredients: 9 ounces of light lead carbonate (WhitePowderedChalk9ozs), 1 ounce of white sugar (WhiteSugerIoz), 1.5 ounces of high-quality olive oil soap powder (PowderedCortileSoapI2\Iozs), 1 ounce of white angelica powder (OrrisRootIoz).

Instructions: After preparing the above ingredients, mix them thoroughly in a bowl. Pour them out onto paper repeatedly, grind them into a fine powder using a clean wine bottle, ensuring that they are finely and evenly mixed. This creates a cheap and high-quality tooth powder that is excellent for cleaning teeth.

Casual Chat

Random Thoughts on Reading

— Bei Lei

(Those who aspire to read lack money, and those who have money to read lack aspiration) is a common ailment of modern youth. We can cry for the former and mourn for the latter.

(Readers dislike exercise, and those who like exercise often don't read) is also one of the defects of modern education. Those who excel in intelligence are poor in physical strength, and those who excel in physical strength are weak in intelligence. Neither can accomplish great things.

(Viewing education as a source of profit and students as fat sheep) is why Chinese education has not been able to develop to this day.

The ancients said (reading to clarify aspirations) and also (reading to understand principles). Hu Shi said (reading for the sake of reading). These are all answers to why one should read. But now there are new interpretations, namely (reading to show off), (reading to pursue the opposite sex), (reading to practice being future politicians and dignitaries), and (reading for romance).

If you give a student a scientific book and ten books on politics and economics, they will always quickly grab the books on politics and economics and run. A volume of Oscar Wilde's English literature is not as popular as one (History of Sexuality).

The more one reads, the less one dares to speak, but what one can say is not refuted. Those who speak a lot and often have limited knowledge.

Drops of Thoughts

— Wu

During the yellow season, I was alone, left behind in front of the gray-white window. The loneliness of wanting to die tightly wrapped me, allowing my mood to remain tranquil, so I was very indulgent towards my own thoughts.

The wealthy family across the street paid a very high price for these beautiful roses, but they couldn't thrive due to the master's kindness. This must have disappointed the rich man too much, right?

However, roses can always be repurchased, even though their thorns sometimes prick your skin.

As long as you have money, you can become an official. Similarly, as long as you are an official, you will make money. Originally, these are two-in-one, one-in-two things.

Some say that the command knife can command scholars, but most of the so-called scholars are happy to be commanded by the command knife.

That's how they depend on each other for survival.

The newspaper reported that (a certain military leader) is going to personally take the field again... But this (command knife) does not announce his full name in advance, but only prefixes it with the word (a certain). Why? I think this is probably because once, twice, three times..., afraid of being asked (Aren't you ashamed?)

Before the white cat left, the mice started fighting again. If they can't decide the winner, they can ask the tabby cat for help.

This is brothers fighting within the walls, defending against external (insults).

The old bully next door was secretly attacked by hooligans. The weak were overjoyed and laughed loudly, but were immediately seen by the bully's godson, who gave the laugher a full slap. I think this was really a satisfying hit; (...Why did you laugh at his stepfather's death in his face? What an idiot!)

…………………………

Suddenly the electric light came on, and the room was filled with white light. My mood was subdued by it and did not dare to tremble.

Must Have

Seeking an Accountant

On the second floor of a large building on Yuanmingyuan Road, a sign from ×× Company was posted on the spring door of the office. I carefully pushed the door open and went in.

("Is this the place that advertised in the newspaper yesterday for an accountant, a debt collector, and several social secretaries?") I cautiously asked a gentleman, about thirty years old, sitting at the writing desk, with a respectful attitude.

"Yes," he replied.

"We are already fully staffed, but there is still a vacancy in the accounting department, with a monthly salary of thirty yuan. Room and board are not provided. In addition to the shop guarantee, a cash guarantee of two hundred yuan is also required," he continued.

At that time, I asked him, since there is a reliable shop guarantee, why is a cash guarantee of two hundred yuan still needed? He said without hesitation, ("Because with a shop guarantee, although there is a possibility of guarantee, if there is a debt of tens or hundreds of yuan to the company, or if a small incident occurs, then it is certainly possible to seek compensation from the guarantor according to the law, but for this small amount of money, hiring a lawyer and paying litigation fees may not be worth the loss. Therefore, after the decision of our company's manager, from now on, in addition to the shop guarantee, new employees must have a considerable cash guarantee.") After hearing his words, I felt that it was fully justified. Just as we were about to continue talking, two young women ran in from outside the door. Sure enough, their mission was also for this matter. He routinely told them about the various treatments and conditions. Later, they asked if the cash guarantee could be reduced. He solemnly stated that there could be no concession, and said that this was the company's regulations. Needless to say, it was all for this matter. Because of time constraints, I wrote down a mailing address and agreed to hear back on Sunday morning. As I left the office, I thought to myself that when I walked in, he didn't say that there was only one vacancy, but later one person came in after another, and he didn't mention that sentence. This is the first suspicious point. Since he advertised in the newspaper for an accountant, he undoubtedly wanted to find suitable talent. He should have given considerable consideration to the employees he hired, whether they could be competent for their responsibilities. But he never paid attention to this point. As long as you have a cash guarantee of two hundred yuan and the ability to get a shop guarantee, you can be hired. This is the second suspicious point.

On Sunday, because I had other things to do, I couldn't go, and later I put this matter aside. About three weeks later, I saw a similar recruitment advertisement in the newspaper's employment section, but his address was at ×× Company on Fuxi Road. The next day, I happened to pass by that location, so I conveniently ran in to inquire. Unexpectedly, as soon as I entered the door, I saw the gentleman who had talked to me on Yuanmingyuan Road before. At the same time, there were several young people who had entered before me. His conversation was exactly the same as what he had said last time. At that time, I became even more suspicious. Last time he said that there was only one vacancy, but there were more than ten times the number of people who went to negotiate that day, and why did he publish such a large recruitment advertisement again? Moreover, recruiting employees is an open and aboveboard matter, so why was the address first on Yuanmingyuan Road and then on Fuxi Road? The background behind it is self-evident.

Written by Feng Nian on the evening of May 13th.

A Corner of Society

A Maid's Confession (2)

— Le Shan

The young girl, about ten years old, of the great-aunt always went out with the madam and young madam every night. Influenced by what she saw and heard, she learned to play roulette. When she came back, she would imitate it, forcibly asking me and ×× to take out our money and play with her. She didn't want copper coins, she had to have silver dollars. Sometimes, she would snatch three or five silver dollars from us and firmly refuse to return them. If we didn't ask her for it, how much would we earn in a month for our hard work? If we asked her for it, she would carelessly poke and throw sharp objects like scissors. We had no choice but to swallow our anger and not dare to confront her fierce edge.

They would rather lose hundreds of silver dollars on roulette than be willing to buy an electric fan. Whenever the fat madam, who was afraid of the heat, reached summer, she would order us to stand behind her and fan her, whether she was eating or playing cards. We kept fanning her continuously, and even though our hands were sore and tired, she would still angrily complain and blame heaven and earth, even rewarding us with a couple of slaps.

The madam wanted to be fanned while eating, and the young master and the great-aunt's little girl also made a fuss about wanting to be fanned. Our two fleshy hands became a strange electric fan that didn't feel tired. We were so busy that we were sweating like rain and had nowhere to go.

In the eyes of ordinary people, maids seem to be lowly and greedy, disregarding shame. Therefore, when the master lost silver coins or valuable things such as jewelry, they suspected that the maids stole them. Our master, who lacked moral instruction and had no ability to judge people, usually guarded against us as strictly as against thieves.

One day, unfortunately, one of the great-aunt's gold rings and one of her bracelets disappeared. The master and madam said in stern voices that we stole them and ordered us to confess. We were so angry that we couldn't open our mouths. They tied us up and beat us, and then conducted a thorough search of our whole bodies and bedding, clothes, and bags, but still couldn't find the stolen goods. They beat us again and insisted that we had taken them out to pawn, forcing us to produce the pawn tickets. At that time, both ×× and I would rather be beaten to death than falsely admit to being thieves.

Although the madam compensated the great-aunt, she felt very pained at the thought of spending two or three hundred yuan, so she vented her anger on us. I was in so much pain that I wanted to commit suicide several times, but I was afraid that dying would only sink me deeper into injustice. Alas! It was so painful to live, and impossible to die, it was truly unbearable!

Heaven has eyes. Later, the young master suddenly contracted syphilis, which became more and more severe every day. He couldn't hide it from the master and madam. After questioning him, they finally realized that it was the dignified young master who stole the gold ring and gold bracelet, not us lowly maids. Only then did their suspicions break and our grievances were cleared.

When Mrs. C heard this, she couldn't help but say ("Amitabha"), causing us to burst into laughter, which interrupted the maid's words. I then got up to say goodbye.

Witty Remarks

— Ze Yong

If college students don't make a stir with student movements, they can't be considered college students.

Having a few star athletes in the school can win a lot of fame for the school.

A strike is when the employees give the boss a break from business.

Talking about chastity with a modern woman is like playing the lute to a cow.

If you have a PhD or master's title, even if you fart, people will say it smells good.

In today's society, if you want to make a living, if you don't know how to perform tricks and tell lies, you will die wronged.

If you don't print a few more titles on your business card, you can't be considered a wealthy official.

Wearing a Chinese long gown but Western-style trousers is the most fashionable outfit now.

A Small Wonder

Humble Later, Arrogant Before

— Nuo Xia

A middle-aged woman said very sincerely to her husband, Mr. Wang:

("Honey, you still have nothing to do today, why don't you come to the company with me to buy something?")

Mr. Wang just sat on the sofa smoking and reading the newspaper, pretending not to hear. It was only after the third question that he put on a smiling face and replied,

("It would be embarrassing for my friends to see me, you should go by yourself.")

She had nothing to say, so she left alone in frustration.

×　　×　　×　　×　　×

Mr. Wang said very sincerely to his lover:

("Are you going to the company to buy something today? Let me go with you.")

His lover just put on makeup in front of the mirror, pretending not to hear. It was only after the third question that she put on a smiling face and replied:

("It would be embarrassing for my sisters to see me, you should just wait at home.")

He had nothing to say. He watched his lover leave, then lay down on the rocking chair and dozed off, waiting for her to return.

The real estate owned by the debtor has been sealed and auctioned. It has now expired and no one has purchased it. Those who are willing to offer a price should submit their name, age, origin, address, occupation, and desired bid in a sealed letter and place it in the bid box. On the due date, the bid will be opened according to law. The bidder with the highest price will be the winning bidder. The winning bidder should pay one-fifth of the bid price as a deposit on the same day, and the remaining amount will be paid in full upon delivery of the property, at which point this court will issue a property management certificate. If payment is not made within the time limit, the bidder with the second highest price among the bidders will be substituted and handled according to the aforementioned procedures. The residents such as Fang Yangmin et al. should be informed, and all interested parties should be present on the day of the bidding to avoid any misunderstandings. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized shall be commuted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment, all with a three-year suspended sentence. Wang Amei and Cheng Ali are both found not guilty. Four opium pipes, four opium lamps, one opium tray, and a small amount of opium residue and red pills are all confiscated.

▲Civil Judgment: Yongfeng & Co., Le Junjin vs. Tan Yigong, goods payment case (Main Text): The defendant should pay the plaintiff goods payment of $52.50; the plaintiff's other claims are dismissed; the plaintiff bears one-third of the litigation costs, and the defendant bears two-thirds. ▲Berly Ming vs. Keli Huafu et al., goods payment case (Main Text): The defendant Keli Huafu should pay the plaintiff $165.90; the defendant Fa Yi Wei Xian Wei Qi should pay the plaintiff $35.40; the litigation costs are borne by the defendants in proportion; this judgment can be executed provisionally. ▲Berly Ming vs. Weilai Er et al., goods payment case (Main Text): The defendant Weilai Er should pay the plaintiff $242.34; Automobile News

Commentary

Investment of 10 Million Dollars for

The 1932 New Car Competition

▲Ford's Grand Plan In the American automobile industry, one recent event has attracted considerable attention. That is, Ford Motor Company's efforts to manufacture new Ford automobiles. According to Ford, the new cars it produces will be shipped to 200 major cities across the United States for public display. Ford's move not only adds a unique color to the American automobile industry but also benefits a large number of unemployed workers. Henry and Edsel Ford's new initiative boldly challenges (the depression) and provides a concrete solution to the unemployment problem. Ford's new eastern plant is located in Edgewater, New Jersey. Although the company is reluctant to disclose the number of employees, it is reliable to say that former workers will be given priority. Currently, Ford employs approximately 70,000 workers, which is estimated to increase to 100,000, and can accommodate up to 120,000 workers at its peak.

Ford's manufacturing of new automobiles requires a considerable amount of working capital, easily amounting to millions of dollars. According to Associated Press news, the expenses include the following: (1) Raw materials, transportation, and labor in Detroit: $300,000,000. (2) Expenses for railway and shipping companies: $86,000,000. (3) Monthly procurement of new raw materials: $52,000,000. (4) Expenses for decoration and fabrics: $48,000,000. (5) Steel materials purchased from the market: $47,000,000. (6) Tires: $20,000,000. (7) Monthly wages for 10,000 workers: $18,000,000. (8) Steel materials manufactured by the plant: $16,000,000. (9) Glass expenses: $10,000,000. (10) Additional machinery: $6,375,000. (11) Malleable cast iron: $5,044,000. (12) Paint: $4,854,000. (13) Raw rubber: $4,800,000. (14) Pig iron: $4,680,000. (15) Hardwood: $4,000,000. (16) Copper: $3,500,000. (17) Lead: $1,500,000. Based on the above quantities, the transportation will require 236,000 inbound vehicles and 228,000 outbound vehicles, which will provide railway personnel with more work and prevent them from being idle.

When announcing the launch of the new car, Edsel Ford, General Manager of Ford Motor Company, stated that his father and he firmly believe that domestic commerce can have some recovery at this time. Ford also said, "We are very clear about the future of the new car. The car we want to build should have eight cylinders and extremely high horsepower, but its structure should be very simple. Its characteristics should be its speed and power, and its selling price should be in line with the public's ability to purchase. I can definitely say that all the costs of building this car are not taken into account, because the more carefully the cost is calculated, the higher the selling price will be. Therefore, the time and effort spent on building the car are not taken into account. We are very aware of our responsibilities and are trying our best to find ways to restore workers to their jobs. This project has already started. Next Thursday, the people of the country can judge our work. In addition to the eight-cylinder and 65-horsepower car, we are also building a four-cylinder and 50-horsepower car. These two types of cars have 14 different styles, but except for the engine, the two cars are generally the same. The car body and frame are absolutely the same, but the selling prices of the two cars are different. The V8 will be listed among the low-priced cars, while the (4) will be even cheaper. This is our aim to serve the driving public, especially in the current economic situation."

American automobile companies have invested heavily in planning their 1932 automobile businesses. The amount of investment has exceeded $1,000,000,000, and many companies have already launched new cars. The progress planned is beyond what has been imagined in recent years. This kind of progress is believed to promote the improvement of business. However, after learning about Ford's plan in February, people inevitably felt a setback. The impact was particularly severe on low-priced cars. Leaders of other automobile companies hoped that this kind of promotion would only allow people to see what the new Ford was like before buying, and that the buying situation would return to normal when it was presented. If this is true, then the launch of Ford's new car can increase general business.

General Motors Company recently established a sales organization to integrate sales and manufacturing. The companies involved are Buick, Oldsmobile, and Pontiac, which are mid-priced cars. Chrysler's Plymouth car was launched on April 3rd. Studebaker and Graham-Paige both stated that sales were very successful. Therefore, the future of various new cars is very bright.

The new Ford V8 can travel 75 miles per hour, and the four-cylinder can travel 65 miles per hour. As for the characteristics of its engine structure, there are also some that can be introduced, such as silent synchronous shifting, silent gears, engine rubber isolation, downdraft carburetor and carburetor silencer, automatic spark management, diaphragm pump to force fuel out of the rear fuel tank. In addition, there are flexible transverse semi-suspended springs, new-style tail springs, self-adjusting double-acting shock absorbers, large four-wheel brakes, new-style electric steel-spoked wheels with large hubs, hubcaps, and large tires. Rubber is used extensively in the new car. Rubber isolation is used in the frame and the spring hooks and shock-absorbing chain links of the running gear to reduce vibration. Rubber is also used as a pad between the car body and the frame.

Streamlining of Transportation Equipment

▲A Great Revolution in the World of Power

Suppose you are driving your current, commonly used car at high speed on the road, traveling at 60 miles per hour. Now, imagine your car suddenly changes: its engine moves to the rear, the flat radiator becomes rounded, and the headlights and bumpers are shrunk and integrated into the smooth, rounded front. The square rear of the car is elongated, trailing into a long, pointed tail.

Now, look at your speedometer. Even though you haven’t pushed the accelerator even a millimeter more, your car's speed has increased from 60 to 75 miles per hour. Simultaneously, while the speed has increased, the gasoline consumption has not increased at all.

This ideal reformation is one of the effects of "streamlining." "Streamline"—readers probably already know—is the route of fluid (like water and air) flow. "Streamlining" means shaping the outline of a moving object in a way that allows fluids to flow smoothly without obstruction, thereby reducing its resistance.

If a car has been properly streamlined, it can travel 35 to 40 miles per gallon of gasoline, at least doubling the mileage compared to using an old-fashioned car. Most current cars have square backs and many protruding parts, all of which obstruct the smooth flow of air, thus subjecting the car to great resistance.

Recently, a type of "teardrop" car has appeared in the United States, attracting general attention and criticism. Everyone thinks that a falling teardrop or raindrop is a perfectly streamlined form. However, Dr. H.L. Dryden, a fluid mechanics expert at the U.S. Bureau of Standards, disagrees. He believes that people tend to overemphasize the teardrop shape and neglect other forms. "In fact," he says, "any shape without edges that cause reverse vortices can be considered streamlined. From a streamlined point of view, the 'teardrop' shape is not necessarily the best." Dr. Dryden also states that partial or superficial streamlining (such as changing square edges to round edges) is ineffective. All automobiles must be remodeled according to principles derived from practical experiments.

The doctor also says that most car drivers do not know that the maximum speed of an ordinary car is limited by air resistance. When the car travels at speeds above 40 or 50 miles per hour, wind resistance becomes the only obstacle. Therefore, reducing this resistance is equivalent to increasing the speed accordingly. The application of streamlining can reduce this resistance by half.

Dr. Dryden further expresses a brilliant insight, stating that while currently so-called streamlined cars can indeed travel twice as far on one gallon of gasoline, their resistance is still ten times greater than that of a completely streamlined car. The attainment of the highest standard awaits the future. At that time, one gallon of gasoline will be able to travel 100 miles or more.

The streamlining of cars involves not only formal modifications but also various fundamental changes, such as moving the engine behind the seats, lowering the seats, reducing the cross-sectional area of the car body, and so on. The result of streamlining will make driving more comfortable and economical because the structure of the car will be simplified. Also, when the car is driving, dust can be prevented from flying behind the car due to the smooth flow of air.

In California, USA, at least six freight trucking routes have already converted their trucks to streamlined forms. As a result, they are able to carry goods up to the legal weight limit with little increase in gasoline consumption. On the roads of Germany, streamlined cars are already common sights. In England, streamlined cars are also gradually becoming visible. Not long ago, Sir Denistoun Burney's airship-like car made its first appearance on British roads. The crowd was amazed by the integrated, beautifully curved machine. Although the car only had 22 horsepower, road tests showed that it could reach a speed of 80 miles per hour. In other countries, the streamlining of cars is receiving similar attention and welcome. (To be continued) News

A Glimpse of the Features of the New Dodge Car

Dodge cars are renowned in the automotive world for their excellent materials. Their manufacturing excellence, vehicle reliability, and beautiful appearance are all praised by society. In a word, everything about Dodge cars is superior to other vehicles, which is generally recognized in the automotive industry. Recently, many new eight-cylinder and six-cylinder Dodge cars have arrived in Shanghai. Therefore, we have studied these new cars one by one, and it is undeniable that the new Dodge cars have their own unique advantages. Tracing back to the source, the Dodge Brothers Motor Company was initially known for manufacturing sturdy, wide-edged small cars. At that time, the sales of these small cars were unprecedented. Since then, new cars have been introduced to the automotive market every year, greatly pleasing car owners. To this day, the value of Dodge cars has become the best in the industry.

Dodge cars are known in the automotive market for their precise construction, as mentioned above. However, the construction of the 1932 model new car is also based on previous examples, with many changes. Moreover, the increase in speed, the improvement in safety, and the beautiful appearance are beyond the reach of previous new cars. In the past, when manufacturing vehicles, the engineering aspects were refined and perfected, sparing no effort. This year's new car has paid even more attention to the internal structure. All the advantages of the past are fully preserved, and the decoration is even more exquisite today. Therefore, the new Dodge car has become the most perfect car today.

The dealer of new Dodge cars is the China Motor Company. People who want to buy a car can go for a test drive day or night. Once the car owner tries it, the advantages of the Dodge car are immediately apparent, such as the automatic engaging clutch, silent gears, and live wheels, which are even more important advantages. As for the richness of power, it is even more unprecedented. Regardless of the six-cylinder or eight-cylinder, it can use an amazing push rod on difficult roads to obtain the fastest speed. In terms of horsepower, it is like a heavenly horse flying in the sky, and it can be active everywhere. When driving in the countryside or on city streets, there is no noise at all. Even using the highest gear, there is no sense of vibration.

The automatic engaging clutch works perfectly with the live wheel system. The live wheel adopts a dual-use type, which is used to handle the engaging clutch. Silent gears are also one of the advantages. When in use, there is no noise under any circumstances. In addition, the hydraulic brake with a temperature indicator is also the latest device. The car body is cast from a single piece of steel, which can increase the car's robustness. Any force cannot damage the car body. The frame is shaped like a bridge, so it can also be used as a racing car on the road. Using the second gear, the speed per hour can also reach 50 miles. In summary, readers can easily understand the advantages of the new Dodge car. Therefore, since the new car was launched, it has become popular all over the world in just a few months.

New Record of Williams-Avellan

Preface

A Williams-Avellan six-cylinder sports car broke the record between New York and Los Angeles by traversing an extremely long distance of the continent at the fastest speed. The return trip time was only seven hours apart.

▲The new record was produced by a long distance of 6,770 miles back and forth between New York and Los Angeles. The new record between the two cities was produced in 135 hours and 22 minutes. The average speed was 50.066 miles per hour, which is the new highest average speed. The former was 47.05 miles. The climate of the trip ranged from hot to watery, rainy and foggy, from sea level to over 8,000 feet above sea level. In order to produce the record, it sometimes traveled more than one mile in one minute.

▲Cross-country rush departed from the Western Union Association west of New York at midnight. The two drivers reached Los Angeles 65 hours and 19 minutes after departure. This itinerary has been completed. This new record from one coast to another is not only the glory of Williams-Avellan, but also the great efforts of the two drivers. Before departure, one of the drivers said, "My intention is to choose a low-priced car for this trip." After researching various low-priced cars, he decided to choose a Williams-Avellan six-cylinder sports car because of its strong structure, high horsepower and safety characteristics.

▲Overcoming dangers In the past, the records between the two cities were produced by cars with higher prices than Williams-Avellan, and with the help of highway experts and police to guide the route and so on. However, this time Williams-Avellan did not have any kind of help, so safety through large cities and rural areas was a major issue. The speed was therefore hindered. The first part of the trip was to pass through the Ali Han Mountains with 440 miles in heavy fog. This section of the road was extremely difficult to do, but it was still able to travel 444 in 7 hours and 49 minutes, with an average speed of 58.7 miles per hour. The 415 miles from Washington to Junsef were reached in 474 minutes. The 415 miles from Spring Land to Tepica in Erlenor were also reached in 474 minutes. There were times when the speed of the car was as fast as 70 miles per hour. Secondly, the 985 miles from Tepica to Earl Punk had extremely winding mountain roads and faced the sea breeze blowing from the Pacific Ocean, and passed through the famous Raton Gorge. It was still rare to be able to complete the journey in 18 hours and 31 minutes, with an average speed of 53.7 miles. This section of the itinerary is indeed enough to prove the reliability of the car's engine power, radiator, and oil system, all of which have given us great satisfaction. 65 hours and 19 minutes after leaving New York, we arrived safely in Los Angeles. After arriving, we inspected all the mechanical parts, and their perfect condition remained the same as before. The next afternoon, we set off again and passed through the desert at night. Later, when we reached Mt. Furnace and Mt. Taff, the temperature dropped to freezing point, and the effect of the car's motor remained the same as before. 45 hours after leaving Los Angeles, we arrived in Petersville. We arrived in Washington at 6:43 the next morning. From here, heading towards New York, the speed gradually decreased, because officials were inspecting the machinery from time to time.

▲Back to New York We safely arrived at the Western Union Association in New York at 3:22 pm. We came out to inspect and verified that the time spent was 135 hours and 22 minutes, which is a new record for the round trip from New York to Los Angeles. A driver said, "Our car was officially inspected at the New York Service Department after arriving, and it was guaranteed that the car's motor still maintained excellent condition after traveling 6,770 miles." According to 1932, it is the 25th anniversary of the Williams-Avellan Company. The Knight and Bobbitt cars manufactured by the company are welcomed all over the world. In the past few years, it has produced several speed and economic records. The price of this year's 1932 car is the lowest in the company's history. Yingtam

British Automotive News Pei

▲British people like to drive children's cars (children's) cars are small criminal cars. Economical cost and convenient driving. All drive big cars and go up. In recent years, British people's trends have shown a fondness for small cars. Therefore, a kind of small car with 8 to 12 horsepower is popular in London. This kind of small car not only saves a lot of fuel, but also has the benefit of reducing taxes and fees. British middle-class people like to buy it the most. All those who used to buy 13, 16 and 20 horsepower cars have changed to use this kind of small car because of the heavy horsepower tax and the high price of fuel. According to London car dealers, the 20 horsepower big cars will gradually decrease in the future. As for the small cars, they are often sold out after they leave the factory. There is a great trend of demand exceeding supply. The difference in the cost of big cars and small cars can be seen from the proportion. For example, if each car travels 7,000 miles a year and each gallon of gasoline costs 3 shillings and 2 pence, the expenses of various sizes of cars are as follows. 8 horsepower, tax 8 pounds, insurance 12 pounds, gasoline 10 pounds and 8 shillings, a total of 30 pounds and 8 shillings. 9 horsepower, tax 9 pounds, insurance 12 pounds, gasoline 11 pounds and 14 shillings, a total of 32 pounds and 14 shillings. 15 horsepower, tax 15 pounds, insurance 15 pounds, gasoline 23 pounds and 7 shillings, a total of 53 pounds and 7 shillings. 20 horsepower, tax 20 pounds, insurance 20 pounds, gasoline 26 pounds and 10 shillings, a total of 66 pounds and 10 shillings. The above tax, insurance, and gasoline are the three prerequisites for driving a car. The 30 pounds and 10 shillings of the 8 horsepower car is one times different compared with the 66 pounds and 10 shillings of the 20 horsepower car. The difference in cost between big and small cars can be understood from this.

▲More British cars exported According to the statistics of the British Ministry of Commerce in March, the number of car exports increased by £11,674 compared with February. However, if compared with the same period in 1931, it fell by £38,475. In total for three months, it decreased by £300,059. The export of complete cars and parts increased by £67,392. The export of car frames increased by £19,279. The total number of motorcycles and parts in March increased by £117,603 compared with February. March of this year increased by £21,074 compared with the same period last year. However, three months decreased by £184,147. Regarding imports, the number this year is less than last year. Compared with the same period last year in March this year, the import of all cars fell by £27,578. The total number of three months decreased by £73.625. The import value of car frames decreased by £14,691 in March this year compared with March 1931. The total of three months fell by £36,115. The number of imported parts increased by £59,980 in March compared with the same period last year. If the total is calculated in three months, it will be less by £35,213. Comparing imports and exports, British car exports exceeded imports by £217,510 in March. The total oversupply for three months was £956,103.

▲Decrease in the number of American-made cars exported to the UK Although the UK manufactures many cars by itself, the number of cars imported from foreign countries in previous years was also quite large. However, last year, due to the UK's change in tax rates and the tendency of buyers to purchase small cars, the number of foreign cars exported to the UK decreased significantly. Among them, the impact of cars made in the United States was even greater. According to statistics, the number of cars shipped from the United States to the United Kingdom last year was only 3,130 units. In 1930, there were 10,694 units. In 1929, there were 22,729 units. Comparing the two, the difference is far away. The reasons for the decline can be roughly divided into four points. 1. Due to the decline of all industries, the economic power of the society is unstable, and buyers are hesitant to move forward. 2. The British pound depreciated, resulting in a huge hidden loss. 3. The import tax on foreign goods has increased. Cars are taxed based on horsepower. 4. British people tend to wear small cars. With the above four relationships, the import of American cars is decreasing day by day. As for horsepower taxation, it is not very high, but the amount of import tax is huge. British people who buy foreign cars are often unwilling to spend extra money. Therefore, when choosing between them, they unconsciously plan a lot for American cars, and replace them with domestic products.

▲Current status of automobile taxation in the UK In 1920, the UK levied the current system of motorcycle tax. In the past twelve years, it has increased from £7,775,000 to £28,000,000. The latest tax revenue, from December 1, 1931 to February 20, 1932, totaled £16,931,359. The same period last year was £16,993,368. Comparing the two, it decreased by £62,000. This is probably the first time that income has decreased since the automobile tax was levied. The tax revenue in 1930 was £16,552,113, and in 1931 it was £16,993,368. Last year increased by £441,255 compared with the previous year. As for the £62,000 that fell from September last year to February this year, it was not because the number of car registrations was small, which affected the tax revenue. In fact, the number of cars has been growing. However, because most buyers choose small cars, the tax they pay also decreases with it. Miscellaneous notes
